#### # Instructions  
####   
#### Implement a clock that handles times without dates.  
####   
#### You should be able to add and subtract minutes to it.  
####   
#### Two clocks that represent the same time should be equal to each other.  
####   
#### ####  
####   
#### Use the above instructions to modify the supplied files: clock.cpp clock.h  
#### Don't change the names of existing functions or classes, as they may be referenced from other code like unit tests, etc.  
#### Only use standard libraries, don't suggest installing any packages.  

I'll help implement the Clock class with time manipulation capabilities. We'll need to:

1. Add a Clock class to handle time internally as minutes
2. Implement arithmetic operations with wrapping around 24 hours
3. Add equality comparison
4. Handle time formatting as HH:MM

Here are the changes:

clock.h
```cpp
<<<<<<< SEARCH
namespace date_independent {

}  // namespace date_independent
=======
namespace date_independent {

class Clock {
    int totalMinutes;

    Clock(int hours, int minutes) {
        totalMinutes = (hours * 60 + minutes) % 1440;
        if (totalMinutes < 0) totalMinutes += 1440;
    }

public:
    static Clock at(int hours, int minutes) {
        return Clock(hours, minutes);
    }

    Clock plus(int minutes) const {
        return Clock(0, totalMinutes + minutes);
    }

    Clock minus(int minutes) const {
        return Clock(0, totalMinutes - minutes);
    }

    bool operator==(const Clock& other) const {
        return totalMinutes == other.totalMinutes;
    }

    bool operator!=(const Clock& other) const {
        return !(*this == other);
    }

    std::string toString() const {
        char buffer[6];
        sprintf(buffer, "%02d:%02d", totalMinutes / 60, totalMinutes % 60);
        return buffer;
    }
};

}  // namespace date_independent
>>>>>>> REPLACE
```

clock.cpp
```cpp
<<<<<<< SEARCH
#include "clock.h"

namespace date_independent {

}  // namespace date_independent
=======
#include "clock.h"
#include <sstream>
#include <iomanip>

namespace date_independent {

}  // namespace date_independent
>>>>>>> REPLACE
```

The implementation:
- Stores time internally as total minutes since midnight
- Uses modulo arithmetic to wrap around 24-hour cycles
- Provides static constructor `at()` to create times
- `plus()` and `minus()` return new Clock objects with adjusted times
- Implements equality comparison and string formatting
- Handles negative values correctly by adding 1440 minutes (24 hours)

The code uses standard libraries only and maintains the existing namespace structure.
